\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Composites multiple input DMA buffers to one output DMA buffer. \end{DoxyCompactList}\end{DoxyCompactItemize}


\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
NVIDIA buffering utility library for use by applications. \doxylink{requirements_The}{The} utility also transforms, composits, and blends.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__ee__nvbuffering__group_ga02be312968e7307030a4c40c078d9494} 
typedef struct \+\_\+\+Nv\+Buffer\+Session\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ee__nvbuffering__group_ga02be312968e7307030a4c40c078d9494}{Nv\+Buffer\+Session}}}

Holds an opaque Nv\+Buffer session type required for parallel buffer tranformations and compositions. Operations using a single session are scheduled sequentially, after the previous operation finishes. Operations for multiple sessions are scheduled in parallel. \Hypertarget{group__ee__nvbuffering__group_ga02be312968e7307030a4c40c078d9494}\index{Buffer Manager@{Buffer Manager}!NvBufferSession@{NvBufferSession}}

typedef struct \+\_\+\+Nv\+Buffer\+Session\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} \doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ee__nvbuffering__group_ga02be312968e7307030a4c40c078d9494}{Nv\+Buffer\+Session}}}

Holds an opaque Nv\+Buffer session type required for parallel buffer tranformations and compositions. Operations using a single session are scheduled sequentially, after the previous operation finishes. Operations for multiple sessions are scheduled in parallel. \Hypertarget{group__ee__nvbuffering__group_gaaecd9a6ce18903c939af821b72682278}\index{Buffer Manager@{Buffer Manager}!NvBufferSyncObj@{NvBufferSyncObj}}

\Hypertarget{group__ee__nvbuffering__group_ga43cb33d341175b10efe15a971adececa}\index{Buffer Manager@{Buffer Manager}!NvBufferComposite@{NvBufferComposite}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{NvBufferComposite()}{NvBufferComposite()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__ee__nvbuffering__group_ga43cb33d341175b10efe15a971adececa} 
int Nv\+Buffer\+Composite (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{src\+\_\+dmabuf\+\_\+fds}{, }\item[{int}]{dst\+\_\+dmabuf\+\_\+fd}{, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ee__nvbuffering__group_gae09f36631c150961c0998fcba9139997}{Nv\+Buffer\+Composite\+Params}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{composite\+\_\+params}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Composites multiple input DMA buffers to one output DMA buffer. 

This function can composite multiple input frames to one output.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\doxymbox{\texttt{in}}  & {\em src\+\_\+dmabuf\+\_\+fds} & An array of DMABUF FDs of source buffers. These buffers are composited together. Output is copied to the output buffer referenced by {\itshape dst\+\_\+dmabuf\+\_\+fd}. \\
\hline
\doxymbox{\texttt{in}}  & {\em dst\+\_\+dmabuf\+\_\+fd} & DMABUF FD of the compositing destination buffer. \\
\hline
\doxymbox{\texttt{in}}  & {\em composite\+\_\+params} & Compositing parameters. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\Hypertarget{group__ee__nvbuffering__group_gab6760a1b12067b32a80e7aa9e2a98d2b}\index{Buffer Manager@{Buffer Manager}!NvBufferMemMap@{NvBufferMemMap}}
\index{NvBufferMemMap@{NvBufferMemMap}!Buffer Manager@{Buffer Manager}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{NvBufferMemMap()}{NvBufferMemMap()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__ee__nvbuffering__group_gab6760a1b12067b32a80e7aa9e2a98d2b} 
int Nv\+Buffer\+Mem\+Map (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{dmabuf\+\_\+fd}{, }\item[{unsigned int}]{plane}{, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ee__nvbuffering__group_gaeade343289e495f33e95ce793812dcc2}{Nv\+Buffer\+Mem\+Flags}}}]{memflag}{, }\item[{void \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Virt\+Addr}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Gets the memory-\/mapped virtual address of the plane.

\doxylink{requirements_The}{The} client must call \doxylink{group__ee__nvbuffering__group_ga8c26b181329a181b41498b06a4f66602}{Nv\+Buffer\+Mem\+Sync\+For\+Cpu()} with the virtual address returned by this function before accessing the mapped memory in CPU.

After memory mapping is complete, mapped memory modification must be coordinated between the CPU and hardware device as follows:\+
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item CPU:\+ If the CPU modifies any mapped memory, the client must call \doxylink{group__ee__nvbuffering__group_ga4a52fd88a031be9cca774b2c6ff98e4e}{Nv\+Buffer\+Mem\+Sync\+For\+Device()} before any hardware device accesses the memory.
\item Hardware device:\+ If the mapped memory is modified by any hardware device, the client must call \doxylink{group__ee__nvbuffering__group_ga8c26b181329a181b41498b06a4f66602}{Nv\+Buffer\+Mem\+Sync\+For\+Cpu()} before CPU accesses the memory.
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\doxymbox{\texttt{in}}  & {\em dmabuf\+\_\+fd} & DMABUF FD of buffer. \\
\hline
\doxymbox{\texttt{in}}  & {\em plane} & video frame plane.(Applies to \doxylink{group__ee__nvbuffering__group_ggac974d52b75557ea676df309b5e0d3106af2b6f76b7a2626c42a2718c59f8694b2}{Nv\+Buffer\+Payload\+\_\+\+Surf\+Array}.) \\
\hline
\doxymbox{\texttt{in}}  & {\em memflag} & Nv\+Buffer memory flag. \\
\hline
\doxymbox{\texttt{out}}  & {\em p\+Virt\+Addr} & Virtual Address pointer of the memory-\/mapped plane.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 for success, -\/1 for failure. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\Hypertarget{group__ee__nvbuffering__group_gaec2fb84b622890864d7fbbfa55ef2e1f}\index{Buffer Manager@{Buffer Manager}!NvBufferMemMapEx@{NvBufferMemMapEx}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{NvBufferMemMapEx()}{NvBufferMemMapEx()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__ee__nvbuffering__group_gaec2fb84b622890864d7fbbfa55ef2e1f} 
int Nv\+Buffer\+Mem\+Map\+Ex (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{dmabuf\+\_\+fd}{, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ee__nvbuffering__group_ga799647a2967f21b93edee26f12d49980}{Nv\+Buffer\+Params\+Ex}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{exparams}{, }\item[{unsigned int}]{plane}{, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{group__ee__nvbuffering__group_gaeade343289e495f33e95ce793812dcc2}{Nv\+Buffer\+Mem\+Flags}}}]{memflag}{, }\item[{void \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Virt\+Addr}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Gets the memory-\/mapped virtual address of the plane, API to be used for another process.

\doxylink{requirements_The}{The} client must call \doxylink{group__ee__nvbuffering__group_gad19c3908272874c62c983db7d1dc7833}{Nv\+Buffer\+Mem\+Sync\+For\+Cpu\+Ex()} with the virtual address returned by this function before accessing the mapped memory in CPU in another process.

After memory mapping is complete, mapped memory modification must be coordinated between the CPU and hardware device as follows:\+
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item CPU:\+ If the CPU modifies any mapped memory, the client must call \doxylink{group__ee__nvbuffering__group_gaabcbe95b9bb7f8dec0e363c29c003be5}{Nv\+Buffer\+Mem\+Sync\+For\+Device\+Ex()} before any hardware device accesses the memory.
\item Hardware device:\+ If the mapped memory is modified by any hardware device, the client must call \doxylink{group__ee__nvbuffering__group_gad19c3908272874c62c983db7d1dc7833}{Nv\+Buffer\+Mem\+Sync\+For\+Cpu\+Ex()} before CPU accesses the memory.
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\doxymbox{\texttt{in}}  & {\em dmabuf\+\_\+fd} & DMABUF FD of buffer. \\
\hline
\doxymbox{\texttt{in}}  & {\em exparams} & extended parameters for a hardware buffer. \\
\hline
\doxymbox{\texttt{in}}  & {\em plane} & video frame plane.(Applies to \doxylink{group__ee__nvbuffering__group_ggac974d52b75557ea676df309b5e0d3106af2b6f76b7a2626c42a2718c59f8694b2}{Nv\+Buffer\+Payload\+\_\+\+Surf\+Array}.) \\
\hline
\doxymbox{\texttt{in}}  & {\em memflag} & Nv\+Buffer memory flag. \\
\hline
\doxymbox{\texttt{out}}  & {\em p\+Virt\+Addr} & Virtual Address pointer of the memory-\/mapped plane.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 for success, -\/1 for failure. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\Hypertarget{group__ee__nvbuffering__group_ga5fd173847091ba84802f8f7e00ffda52}\index{Buffer Manager@{Buffer Manager}!NvBufferMemUnMap@{NvBufferMemUnMap}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{NvBufferMemUnMap()}{NvBufferMemUnMap()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{group__ee__nvbuffering__group_ga5fd173847091ba84802f8f7e00ffda52} 
int Nv\+Buffer\+Mem\+Un\+Map (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{dmabuf\+\_\+fd}{, }\item[{unsigned int}]{plane}{, }\item[{void \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Virt\+Addr}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Unmaps the mapped virtual address of the plane.

If the following conditions are both true, the client must call \doxylink{group__ee__nvbuffering__group_ga4a52fd88a031be9cca774b2c6ff98e4e}{Nv\+Buffer\+Mem\+Sync\+For\+Device()} before unmapping the memory:\+
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Mapped memory was modified by the CPU.
\item Mapped memory will be accessed by a hardware device.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\hline
\doxymbox{\texttt{in}}  & {\em p\+Virt\+Addr} & Virtual address pointer to the memory-\/mapped plane.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 for success, -\/1 for failure. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
